FNV NATIVE SUN LIGHT DEEP CONTRACT AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which native function writes or reads Sky +0x60/+0x6C/+0xC0 sun color fields?
2. Does Sun +0x1C equal Main +0x1C directional light, and is either render-owned?
3. Does any render path write/read NiDirectionalLight +0xD4 diffuse or +0xF0 direction?
4. Are globals 0x012023F4/0x012023F8 only screen-space sun coordinates?

Compatibility rule:
Use a final renderer-owned field for PSY_SunColor/PSY_SunDirection only after this output proves ownership and lifetime. Otherwise keep existing CPU-projected sun data and do not copy NVR raw TESWeather color walking.

Candidate fields from NewVegasReloaded source to prove, not assume:
  Sky +0x28: Sun*
  Sky +0x60/+0x64/+0x68: sunAmbient candidate
  Sky +0x6C/+0x70/+0x74: sunDirectional candidate
  Sky +0xC0/+0xC4/+0xC8: sunFog candidate
  Sun +0x1C: NiDirectionalLight* candidate
  Main +0x1C: NiDirectionalLight* candidate
  Main +0x68: Sky* candidate
  NiLight +0xC4: dimmer
  NiLight +0xC8/+0xD4/+0xE0: ambient/diffuse/specular color
  NiDirectionalLight +0xF0: direction
